		allow = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = ev_homeless_ship_war
			}
			owner = {
				fail_text = {
					text = ev_ai.9005.b.allow
					check_variable = {
						which = ev_unity_stockpile
						value >= ev_unity_income
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { fleet = { fleet_event = { id = ev_ai.9004 } } }
		name = ev_ai.9005.c
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				unity = -1
				mult = ev_unity_income
			}
			
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ev_homeless_ship_war 
			multiplier = 1
			days = 3600
		}
	}

	option = { 
		custom_tooltip = ev_homeless_boom_effect_new
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_technology = tech_homeless_production_resources_1
			}
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				fail_text = {
					text = ev_ai.9005.b.allow
					check_variable = {
						which = ev_unity_stockpile
						value >= ev_unity_income
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { fleet = { fleet_event = { id = ev_ai.9004 } } }
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				unity = -1
				mult = ev_unity_income
			}
		}
		root = {
			fleet = {
				random_combatant_fleet = {
					destroy_fleet = this
				}
			}
			destroy_ship = this
		}
		name = ev_ai.9005.d
		
	}

	option = { 
		custom_tooltip = ev_set_cloaking_active_effect_yes
		trigger = {
			fleet = {
				is_cloaked = no
			}
		}
		allow = {
			
		}
		fleet = {
			set_cloaking_active = yes
		}
		name = ev_ai.9005.e
		hidden_effect = { fleet = { fleet_event = { id = ev_ai.9004 } } }
	}

	option = { 
		custom_tooltip = ev_set_cloaking_active_effect_no
		trigger = {
			fleet = {
				is_cloaked = yes
			}
		}
		allow = {
			
		}
		fleet = {
			set_cloaking_active = no
		}
		name = ev_ai.9005.f
		hidden_effect = { fleet = { fleet_event = { id = ev_ai.9004 } } }
	}
